## File: `core/agent.py`
### Classes
- **`class AgentController`**
  * `def __init__(self, cfg, callbacks)`
  * `def _project_root(self)`
  * `def _init_services(self)` - *Explicitly initialize all service attributes — no magic __getattr__ delegation.*
  * `def _import_and_build(module_path, class_name)`
  * `def _emit_tokens_used(self, prompt_tokens, completion_tokens, provider, model)`
  * `def stop(self)` - *Interrupt and stop agent execution.*
  * `def _is_interrupted(self)`
  * `def shutdown(self)` - *Release service resources (DB connections, etc.).*
  * `def _transition_to(self, new_state, reason)` - *Transition agent to a new state with logging.*
  * `def _persist_run_state(self, user_prompt, has_execution)` - *Persist long-term memory (structured, no raw tool output) + conversation history.*
  * `def _configure_pipeline(self)` - *Auto-detect build/lint commands from the project (legacy — kept for backward compat).*
  * `def _runtime_verify_files(self, modified_files)` - *Per-file runtime verification: syntax + import check cho từng file.*
  * `def _has_leaked_code(self, text)` - *Return True if AI response contains large markdown code blocks or raw HTML source instead of tool tags.*
  * `def _is_awaiting_user_input(self, text)` - *Detect if AI is asking user a question or waiting for selection.*
  * `def _is_conversational_response(self, text, modified_files)` - *Detect if AI response is purely conversational (greeting, explanation) with no actionable work.*
  * `def _extract_plan_steps(self, approved_plan)` - *Parse top-level plan steps — ưu tiên hierarchical plan (active milestone tasks).*
  * `def _build_plan_review_retry_message(self, plan_steps, reason)` - *Ask the AI to reconcile actual work against the approved plan before DONE.*
  * `def _validate_plan_review(self, ai_msg, plan_steps, modified_files)` - *Validate whether the AI reconciled the approved plan before finishing.*
  * `def _build_plan_guard_prompt(self, approved_plan)` - *Build upfront execution instructions for plan reconciliation.*
  * `def _build_task_review_retry_message(self, modified_files, reason)` - *Ask the AI to provide a concrete completion review before DONE.*
  * `def _validate_task_review(self, ai_msg, modified_files, results)` - *Validate the generic completion contract before accepting DONE.*
  * `def _build_completion_guard_prompt(self)` - *Build the generic DONE contract prompt.*
  * `def _summarize_previous_execution(self, prev_messages, prev_modified_files)`
  * `def _check_cross_file_consistency(self, modified_files)` - *Check that multi-file edits haven't broken cross-file references.*
  * `def _smart_truncate(text, max_len)` - *Cắt text tại ranh giới tự nhiên (paragraph/line), không cắt giữa code block.*
  * `def _repair_json(raw)` - *Sửa lỗi JSON phổ biến của LLM: trailing comma, missing quotes, etc.*
  * `def _extract_hierarchical_plan(self, plan_text)` - *Parse JSON từ response LLM → (HierarchicalPlan, raw_json_string).*
  * `def _render_hierarchical_plan(self, hp)` - *Chuyển HierarchicalPlan → Markdown hiển thị cho user.*
  * `def _get_epic_anchor(self)` - *Lấy Epic (mục tiêu tối cao) để ghim vào context.*
  * `def _get_active_tasks_text(self)` - *Lấy tasks của milestone hiện tại để inject vào context.*
  * `def _advance_milestone(self)` - *Chuyển sang milestone tiếp theo. Trả về True nếu còn milestone, False nếu hết.*
  * `def _format_plan_window(self, plan_text, max_steps_display)` - *If using hierarchical plan: show Epic + only current milestone's tasks.*
  * `def _progressive_context_condense(self, iteration, messages, modified_files, total_tokens, approved_plan, user_prompt)` - *Condense early messages and re-inject original goal for long-running tasks.*
  * `def _build_signal_context(self, quality_report)` - *Collect all signals → rank → cap → format context string.*
  * `def _build_context(self, user_prompt)` - *Build project context with long-term memory from past tasks.*
  * `def _format_depgraph_context(self, user_prompt)` - *Dependency Graph context injection — tìm file liên quan đến prompt,*
  * `def _check_semantic_damage(self, modified_files, iteration)` - *So sánh AST trước và sau khi write, phát hiện function/class bị xoá + export break.*
  * `def _should_load_design_system(self)` - *Check if the project has web UI files (HTML, TSX, JSX, CSS).*
  * `def _get_project_tree(self, max_depth)` - *Build a compact project tree (depth 3) showing directory structure.*
  * `def _is_vague_request(self, prompt)` - *Check if a request is too vague for auto execution.*
  * `def _cli_plan_approval(self, plan_text)` - *CLI fallback plan approval (used outside TUI).*

## File: `core/agent_tools.py`
### Classes
- **`class ToolExecutorMixin`** - *Mixin providing _execute_tool via ToolRegistry + individual executors.*
  * `def _init_tool_registry(self)` - *Create and populate the ToolRegistry with all known tools.*
  * `def _execute_tool(self, tc)` - *Execute a single tool call via the ToolRegistry.*
  * `def _validated_write(self, path, content)` - *Pre-commit validation: parse AST/syntax TRƯỚC khi ghi file.*
  * `def _execute_write_file(self, tc)`
  * `def _write_file_chunked(self, path, content)` - *Split large content into section-marked chunks, write skeleton + each section.*
  * `def _execute_patch_file(self, tc)`
  * `def _execute_line_patch(self, tc)`
  * `def _execute_anchor_patch(self, tc)` - *Execute an anchor-based patch — safe section replacement.*
  * `def _execute_run_command(self, tc)`
  * `def _execute_read_file(self, tc)`
  * `def _execute_search_code(self, tc)`
  * `def _execute_debug_error(self, tc)`
  * `def _execute_refactor(self, tc)` - *Execute a multi-file refactor with atomic rollback.*
  * `def _rollback_refactor(self, backups)` - *Restore files to their pre-refactor state.*
  * `def _snapshot_before_write(self, path)` - *Snapshot current file content before modification.*
  * `def _execute_rollback(self, tc)` - *Restore the most recent snapshot from rollback stack.*
  * `def _execute_codebase_outline(self, tc)` - *Return project outline: file paths + classes/functions (no code).*
  * `def _execute_search_replace_block(self, tc)` - *Parse Aider-style SEARCH/REPLACE blocks and apply each as a patch.*

- **`class Intent`**
- **`class PlanContinuationIntent`** - *Intent khi user đang response lại một plan đã có.*
- **`class IntentResult`**
- **`class IntentRouter`** - *Routes user prompts to 6 intents. Zero regex false positives.*
  * `def classify(self, prompt, context_prompt)` - *Fast path: n-gram phrases + deny list. Returns low confidence for LLM path.*
  * `def parse_llm_response(self, raw)` - *Parse LLM JSON response into IntentResult with strict validation.*
  * `def classify_plan_continuation(self, prompt, plan_summary)` - *Fast path: n-gram check first, fallback returns 'other' for LLM to decide.*
  * `def parse_plan_continuation(self, raw)` - *Parse LLM response for plan continuation intent (expects 'execute'/'modify'/'cancel'/'other').*
  * `def _match_ngram(self, phrase, words)` - *Check if phrase appears as consecutive words in the word list.*

## File: `core/services/long_memory.py`
### Classes
- **`class Event`**
- **`class Task`**
- **`class Knowledge`**
- **`class LongMemory`** - *SQLite + FTS5 based long-term memory system.*
  * `def __init__(self, project_root)`
  * `def conn(self)` - *Thread-safe SQLite connection — creates a new one per thread using thread local storage.*
  * `def _ensure_schema(self)` - *Create tables and FTS indexes if they don't exist.*
  * `def close(self)`
  * `def log_event(self, action, file, command, summary, details, task_id)` - *Log a single event. Returns the event ID.*
  * `def log_file_event(self, action, file_path, summary, task_id)` - *Convenience: log a file-related event.*
  * `def log_command_event(self, command, summary, task_id)` - *Convenience: log a command execution event.*
  * `def get_events(self, limit, action, file, task_id)` - *Get events with optional filters.*
  * `def count_events(self)`
  * `def start_task(self, name, files)` - *Start a new task. Returns the task ID.*
  * `def complete_task(self, name, files, result, lessons, summary_md)` - *Complete a task in one call (creates + completes).*
  * `def get_tasks(self, limit, result)` - *Get tasks with optional result filter.*
  * `def get_task(self, task_id)`
  * `def count_tasks(self)`
  * `def add_knowledge(self, pattern_name, pattern_text, source_task_id)` - *Add or update a knowledge pattern.*
  * `def get_knowledge(self, limit)`
  * `def count_knowledge(self)`
  * `def search(self, query, limit)` - *Search across events, tasks, and knowledge using FTS5.*
  * `def _keyword_search(self, query, limit)` - *Fallback keyword search using LIKE queries.*
  * `def _clean_fts_query(self, query)` - *Clean query for FTS5 — remove special characters, use OR for broader matching.*
  * `def build_context_for_query(self, query, max_tokens)` - *Build a focused context string for AI based on a search query.*
  * `def export_task_markdown(self, task_id)` - *Export a task as Markdown.*
  * `def export_knowledge_markdown(self)` - *Export all knowledge as a Markdown document.*
  * `def get_stats(self)` - *Get memory statistics.*
  * `def _row_to_event(self, row)`
  * `def _row_to_task(self, row)`
  * `def _row_to_knowledge(self, row)`

  * `def record(self, error_text, category, attempt, root_cause)` - *Ghi nhận một lỗi và kiểm tra loop.*

  * `def reset(self)` - *Reset toàn bộ state (khi chuyển task).*
  * `def total_attempts(self)`
  * `def _check(self)` - *Kiểm tra 4 điều kiện và trả về kết quả.*
  * `def _check_consecutive(self)` - *Đếm số lần hash giống nhau liên tiếp từ cuối.*
  * `def _check_cycle(self)` - *Kiểm tra xem M lần gần nhất có xoay vòng giữa 2-3 hash không.*
  * `def _check_root_cause(self)` - *Đếm số lần cùng root_cause xuất hiện trong history window.*
  * `def _hash(text)` - *Hash error message để so sánh (bỏ qua số dòng, số byte cụ thể).*

## File: `core/services/section_parser.py`
### Classes

- **`class ParsedFile`** - *A file parsed into sections.*
  * `def get_section(self, name)` - *Get a section by name (case-insensitive).*
  * `def get_section_names(self)` - *Return list of all section names in order.*
  * `def replace_section(self, name, new_content)` - *Replace a section's content and return the full file content.*
  * `def rebuild_with_section(self, name, new_content)` - *Replace section content, preserving markers and surrounding code.*
- **`class SectionParser`** - *Parses files into named sections using comment markers.*
  * `def __init__(self)`
  * `def parse(self, file_path, content)` - *Parse a file's content into sections.*
  * `def inject_section_markers(self, content, section_name, language)` - *Add section markers around the entire content (for first-time setup).*
  * `def suggest_sections(self, file_path, content)` - *Analyze a file and suggest logical section names.*
  * `def auto_section_content(self, content, file_path, min_lines, min_chars)` - *Auto-split large content into named sections with markers.*
  * `def _ext_to_lang(ext)`
  * `def _marker_line(name, kind, lang)` - *Generate a section marker line for the given language.*
  * `def _sectionize_html(self, content, lines)` - *Split HTML into sections at major structural tags only.*
  * `def _sectionize_python(self, content, lines)` - *Split Python into sections at top-level class/function definitions.*
  * `def _sectionize_css(self, content, lines)` - *Split CSS into sections at comment blocks or major rulesets.*
  * `def _sectionize_js(self, content, lines)` - *Split JS/TS into sections at top-level function/class/export.*
  * `def _sectionize_by_size(self, content, lines)` - *Fallback: split by line count when no semantic sections found.*
  * `def _make_section(self, name, lines, idx)` - *Build a section dict from lines (markers added later by language).*
  * `def build_skeleton(self, sections)` - *Build a skeleton file with only section markers.*
